padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1540531">Claudiaandras13</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-13">11/13/24 12:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is not the fresh, nor the delicate, nor the soapy rose. It is sweet and seductive, and simply delicious. Atomic Rose is my fave so far, although I wish it would last longer than 5 hours. I like the dry-down, which is warm and cosy, and more male than unisex (normally not something I would go for).<br />
<br />
Because of the moderate longevity, this fragrance is overpriced. An extrait concentration would be absolutely fabulous.<br />
<br />
I want to mention the following though: when testing a fragrance, I only apply one spray on each wrist and one spray on my chest. With really heavy and long lasting fragrances, this means over spraying. In the case of Atomic Rose, 3 sprays is not that strong and not that long lasting either.<br />
<br />
It does last long on clothes. It has been 3 days since I tested this fragrance, and my coat still smells of Atomic Rose.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2347833"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2347833#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2345216" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
There’s no tartness/pissiness to this. Even with rose, there’s no vintage lean to it. There’s depth, no jaggedness. I feel clean AF wearing this. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1977843">MellieW</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 06:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is beautiful. I will say, use less than you think you need - The first time I wore it I couldn't smell it enough so I sprayed a few extra times before I left home. But it grows as it sits and warms up with your body chemistry and lasts for hours; luckily it wasn't an office day or we'd have needed to open windows. But it isn't unpleasant in the slightest. It's warm, spicy, just the tiniest bit sweet as it dries down and very fresh rose forward (not funeral arrangement roses or synthetic). The boldness and staying power reminds me of Delina, but this is deeper and not as cloying. I personally wouldn't wear this in the dead of summer or to the gym, but others could pull it off. Another win from Initio, although Psychedelic Love is still my favorite by them.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2295604"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2295604#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2292137" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2265405"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2265405#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2261161" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2261161" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jaelzion"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1945282"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1945282.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jaelzion" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2261161ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2261161" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1945282">Jaelzion</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-26">08/26/24 00:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance greets you with a soft, sweet, and musky rose that immediately feels cozy and comforting, like wrapping yourself in a plush velvet blanket. It’s reminiscent of Velvet Petals from Victoria's Secret, but with an added rose twist that gives it a more sophisticated edge. There’s a sheerness to the scent that keeps it from being overpowering, making it perfect for those who might be new to rose fragrances but want to explore this classic note.<br />
<br />
The pink pepper stands out just enough to add a bit of intrigue, without taking away from the overall softness. It’s a rose scent that’s undeniably floral, yet it’s more approachable and lighter compared to something like Lust in Paradise, which leans heavier on the rose. This one feels like an easy introduction to Rose, offering a beautiful balance between the familiar and the refined.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2261161"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2261161#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2244214" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; As other reviews state, it is indeed a lot less screechy and lacks that fruity twang delina has which I'm not a fan of. It resembles OG Delina way more than exclusif, I barely get any exclusif here. Does not resemble the intense cafe scent profile much, the only reason thats in the reminds me section is bc theres rose, in which respect id say this is much closer to something like CH very good girl. The rose in intense cafe style ones also smell very middle eastern...Atomic rose is rather western. I've only smelt lattafa amethyst once or twice but from what I recall it did smell a lot like this or atleast deliver the same vibe. I've had this sitting for ages now and this was my literal second time spraying it, but I gave it a full wear at home and the performance is very impressive, projects really well and the quality is LUSH! Crisp whiffs of fresh, tart rose thats well rounded and smooth. I feel on its own this is a little too simple for me, I layered it with kayali vanilla royale (sugary vanillic oud) and it really added that wow factor- I'm afraid this is the only way I'll be wearing this now on haha</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />

By the way, for the guys afraid of rose, ladies often find it intriguing. <br />

<br />

Longevity 9.5/10<br />
Projection 9/10<br />
Price 2/10<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2140989">Om3r_perfumes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 01:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A recent scent I purchased for my mother. Initio’s Atomic Rose starts off with a very fresh start due to that bergamot note. Slowly that rose and jasmine kicks in. That heavy rose note makes it a feminine fragrance, I feel like initially it starts to lean feminine. However, once the dry down of the base note comes with that vanilla and amber I do think that it becomes more unisex. The dry down is exceptional, the vanilla and amber note combination is always very likable. <br />
<br />
Initio’s Atomic Rose has a strong projection and does last forever. I sprayed this 18 hours ago and I can still smell it on my cloth. This scent is extremely versatile, due to its fresh bergamot start I can see this being worn during the summer. The heavy rise notes makes it a scent that can be worn in the spring. And obviously the dry down of vanilla and amber makes it a night time, winter and fall season scent. <br />
<br />
My one complaint for this fragrance is that it comes at a high price point. In my opinion I think that this smells quite similiar to Soo blue from mancera which comes at half the price. So I do think that there are better alternatives. Also since this is a more feminine scent I won’t be wearing this one, I did get it for my mother at the end of the day. So that also slightly deducts my score. But the scent is still amazing.<br />
<br />
Scent: 9<br />
Projection: 8<br />
Longevity: 10<br />
Value: 6<br />
Overall: 8.5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2177356"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2177356#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176628" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Bergamot doesn’t account for the prominent citrus element in this blend. Hints at Delina and Baccarat but better than both. I don’t pick up on much vanilla but it’s there. Mainly a sweet astringent citrus rose with subtle green facets. There’s some sourness but it’s slight, I speculate it’s from a lime note or some specific terpene that exhibits a sour citrus aroma. <br />

I know some Initios can be a bit questionable when it comes to performance/value for money/reformulations but even in its current state Atomic Rose is very very good. I believe it’s currently 80% vol? What I love about this (and the same with Paragon for me) is that I can smell it on myself all day. Everytime I move my head or walk into a room I just get the most beautiful whiff. It is a deep rose, and is complemented with bergamot and vanilla. Much jammier than Delina and nowhere near as powdery. I agree it’s perfect for all seasons and you can dress it down (less sprays) for casual or dress it up (heavier sprays) for an evening out or date. I find it to be perfectly unisex. I thought, I am going to go into debt trying to obtain all three with these prices. Well, while Musk Therapy was not as I would have hoped, I did obtain a bottle of both Side Effect and then Atomic Rose.<br />
 <br />
Atomic Rose: such a wonderful, delightful rose, vanilla-ish, bright, peppery aroma that radiates from this fragrance. Now, this is a fragrance that has an intense rosy - vanilla combination, yet with a very masculine edge (as stated by Jeremy from Redolessence). Many would think that the Rose in this would give off such a fragrant, venturing into feminine territory, however this does not. The bergamot, citrus, and amber elements prevents that, yet allows for there to be such distinction with the varying audiences that choose to wear this.  (I believe it is a unisex fragrance and anybody can rock this.) I will be ROCKing the absolute snot outta this fragrance. :) Overall, an amazing fragrance!<br />
<br />
Performance: 9/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Sillage: 8/10<br />
Compliment: Wife loves it. Definitely a compliment magnet.<br />
Overall: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2120429"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2120429#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2118567" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1520411">Natizinha77</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-13">03/13/24 10:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume arrived like an hour ago and I opened the box in anticipation. I already have some fragrances from Initio, for example, Absolute Aphrodisiac, Narcotic Delights, Paragon and Psychedelic Love. All of them are lovely and all of them have won my heart. <br />
Atomic Rose is a wondeful rose fragrance (you need to be into rose perfumes!) that is not too cloying because the warmth and sweetness are broken by bergamot. It reminds me of Lady Vengeance by Juliette Has a Gun, but the latter is much more synthetic and artificial. I do know perhaps more natural rose-smelling perfumes, for example Rouge Velours by YSL which is another very pretty rose perfume, this time with white tea and patchouli. AR makes me think of thick, dark-red rose petals warmed by afternoon sun, dipped in dark honey but sprinkled with drops of morning mist sitting on bergamot flowers. A comfort smell, suitable for many different ocassions, should perform well also in higher temperatures. Use sparingly as it is a potent juice!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2091360"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2091360#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2091301" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1961281">2bClare</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-05">03/05/24 05:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To me this is a hot and sweet rose scent. By hot I mean literal temperature, if you could smell that. Some perfumes, mainly Iris, are cold. Atomic Rose is heat and sugar, a bit too much sugar for me, if I’m honest. The heat probably comes from the citrus and pepper.  There is an element of sweetness and powder from the vanilla. The rose is intense but it doesn’t have that velvety dense red feeling, it’s more of a hot pink rose. I find it a little bit sharp and dry instead of round and unctuous, like some roses. I actually think “Hot Pink” would have been a great name for this. Or “Stiletto”.  It’s very well blended and pretty consistent although the dry down is a little more pepper, a little less rose. I think this is a perfume for a younger person, out with friends in summer or going to a club.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2082823"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2082823#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2070597" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2068599" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="HDM80"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1785365"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1785365.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="HDM80" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2068599ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2068599" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1785365">HDM80</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-20">02/20/24 14:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As a man who is not drawn to wearing traditionally “feminine” scents, I am surprised to say I love this fragrance on me. The name could not be more appropriate. This is a BOMB of clean and velvety rose petals, with dark ambers, smooth and slightly sweet vanilla, deep spicy pepper and occasionally sharp, but not overpowering citrus; all blended to the point where you can detect each note smoothly playing into the next. I sprayed one spray on my knee to test on skin while at home. 40 minutes later and fully clothed in 32 degree weather, the silage was BOOMING. The drydown begins at about the 5 hour mark. I began to notice the citrus transitioning to the forefront, creating a fresher and less floral scent. The rose becomes a bit more of a green rose stem vibe, but it’s still waltzing around making its presence known. In the end, this fragrance just has “that thing” that just makes you keep coming back. I picture this as a sexy summer date fragrance for myself. Dressed well in tailored slacks that expose my ankles, silk shirt with top 3 buttons unbuttoned, gold jewelry, playing the role of Romeo. Although I will likely find any reason to wear this, it is THAT GOOD. This is feminine leaning for sure, but a well groomed/dressed man will have the ladies thinking of valentines day with this one. Im sure id love it on a lady also. Lasts all day with depth and projects for about 8 hours! The balance of warmth and freshness makes this an all season fragrance. Definitely a bit much for office, but perfect for date nights and nights out imo. 3-4 sprays max! Great stuff!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2068599"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2068599#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2064245" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It lasted on her all day, creating an atmosphere around her that you could not escape, this absolute beast of a scent projects constantly for hours. <br />

<br />
Cleaner sister to Jo Malone Velvet Rose and Out. Delina without the milky and sugar.<br />
<br />

Now I don't reccomend doing that ever but I did my research of all the perfumes people are comparing this to and I love all of those so I knew there would be a good chance of me liking this. This is elegant and not many sprays are needed because this is a more synthetic smelling scent. I love synthetic smelling scents especially because they last all day on me, think brands like Mancera or Montale. You need to like rose to like this because that is what you will be smelling but it is blended very nice with Egyptian jasmine with the vanilla lingering far in the background to give it some sweetness. Delina is sweeter and fruitier for sure. Atomic rose is definitely a true floral with some vanilla to make it mass pleasing. Super happy to have bought this and the bottle will last me a lifetime. A lot of people claim this is a special event perfume which I can see but I wear this whenever I want with 1 spray behind my neck and 1 spray on each wrist. Creates a nice casual scent bubble around you with jeans and a white tee. Im here to say it's okay to wear your perfumes anytime or place or simply because you want to. There are no rules.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="2007831"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=2007831#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2007760" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; (942902, October 2019, 70ml left for USD 110 - First Impression)<br />
<br />
This one doesn't smell like I am expected.<br />
Because Million Information always refers this to Delina.<br />
Slightly more often than Hibicus Mahajad or Very Good Girl.<br />
<br />
I think this is the most far behind Delina than Hibicus Mahajad even Very Good Girl.<br />
Don't blast me for this but I think this is leans TOY BOY by Moshino (Ambery Citrus + Rose).<br />
This totally lacks all the fruity nuance that make Delina special.<br />
<br />
The scent can be described as sort of slightly dry rose on Citrus Amber (sort of Tygar).<br />
The blends, I would agree this is seamless but the scent is not very detailed.<br />
<br />
I feel let down a bit but the scent do have potential in his regards.<br />
I will ware again and provide further updates.<br />
<br />
But one thing I can be sure that this first batch as the name suggest.<br />
This is total Atomic, it is very strong. It think even stronger than Hibicus Mahajad extrait. <br />
Also, the scent is even more leans Masculine than Hibicus Mahajad.<br />
Which I personally consider more masculine than Delina already (due to leather/green dry down).<br />
<br />
First Impression score : 6/10<br />
<br />
Further update, a few hours pass.<br />
<br />
I kinda understand Delina comparision. It is kinda there.<br />
But it lacks all the fruity. Can be a good thing depends on your POV.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1992777"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1992777#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1987570" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1174774">Anamandy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-28">11/28/23 15:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I thought this was going to be a silage bomb, but it is not in the least. It is a big fragrance for sure, but not like some others I've experienced or own. This smells to me like a jammy, syrupy rose on the line of Nina Ricci Rose L'Estase, Stella McCarthy (though that does this profile much better), and Oud Satin Mood. It has a sweet profile, yet it is not sickly sweet as some jammy rose fragrances can be - looking at you Nina). I'm not adverse to that as I like wearing that profile on occasion, but I have to be in the mood for it. And since I already have Stella, I don't need this. Seriously, there are comparative perfumes at a much cheaper price point than the ridiculous $200 plus they are asking for a bottle of this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1815219">astrorocks</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-28">10/28/23 14:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have, for a very long time, been searching for a rose perfume I like. Generally, I do NOT get along with rose scents and I can't put my finger on why. But I am very, very picky with roses even when they are the background singer in the perfume instead of the main-stage diva. This is rose in a bottle and I LOVE it (FINALLY!). I think the key is the other notes in the perfume, particularly vanilla and jasmine, which I know are some of my favorites. The other thing helping here is it is very very rose-y on my skin. While it isn't single note, the rose absolutely shines through and, for some reason, with florals I tend to really prefer simpler, more singular notes and less complexity. I do get a hit of vanilla that sweetens it up and seems to help 'smooth' the perfume in some way so it doesn't tickle my nose at all (not the easiest task - I am fairly sensitive). Probably (especially) the lack of a musk base helps here, too, because I also don't get along with musks. I tend to prefer any other bases to musks and I really love ambers and ouds. What I'm debating is if it is worth the hefty price tag or not, but given that it's the first of many rose perfumes I kept wanting to spray it probably is for me. I would give this a solid 8.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1963077"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1963077#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1960653" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; As in nuclear explosion.  I don't know many notes and I'm not as well school as many on this site.  However, the first whiff of this perfume near gave me a headache!  That has never happened before with a floral fragrance.  If you can get over the first fifteen minutes, the assault on your senses calms down.  So I would suggest NOT sniffing this for at least fifteen minutes unless you like truly powerful scents.  The lasting power is impressive, which can be a good or bad thing based on your tolerance for strong scents.  I really wanted to love this as it got great reviews.  But it was just too strong for me and I love me a good projecting rose scent.  I have tested approximately 10 rose perfumes to date and this has been the strongest of them all.  On the other end of the spectrum, there is a la rose by MFK.  Lovely, fresh, and realistic but the weakest.  Just tried Rose Gourmand by Zara and as other reviewer stated the promising initial rose scent, it dried down to just vanilla. Rose Magnetic also lost its rose scent after about an hour or so.  So still on the hunt for that perfect, fresh true rose scent that brings a smile to my face.  I have about 50 rose bushes, all of which have amazing scents.  So I do know what roses, as least English and Damascus, smell like.  I may tried Elie Saab's No 1 Rose next.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1955530"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1955530#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1953844" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; By best, I refer both to the scent and the performance of the scent! Masterpiece!! <br />
<br />
I know some will disagree with this statement but this is my opinion on Atomic Rose. <br />
<br />
A nuclear, deep, rich rose with pink pepper and  bergamot in the opening. Add to these, jasmine, vanilla and amber and you have the best rose centric fragrance on the market. I said it again!!<br />
<br />
I have several rose forward fragrances in my collection, some very popular, some less popular, but all good quality. This is  still number 1 for me after several years. <br />
<br />
This is for me what Delina or Delina Exlusive is for the majority of the people. Those 2 seem to get most of the hype nowadays when people discuss rose fragrances.<br />
<br />
I think that Atomic Rose is one of the few fragrances that deserves the hype. Or more hype. Is that good!<br />
<br />
Is it expensive? Surely, it is! But it’s so potent that unless it’s the only rose fragrance in your  collection, or your signature scent, you don’t need to buy a second bottle. A very few sprays and you’re good for the entire day! No joke..</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1939221"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1939221#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1936260" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This comes from a person that finds Delina not that pleasant smelling (I find it too earthy somehow). On the other hand, I see the similarities because they are both rose centered fragrances.<br />
<br />
Atomic Rose is a seductive rose (specific to the Initio house), smooth, dark and feminine and an overall silent killer. I find it to be mature, but that doesn't mean that it's destined for older women in any case. It is mature as in "sensual" mature, "intoxicating" mature.<br />
<br />
I find the color of the bottle to represent the essence of the perfume very well - dark purple velvet. To me it screams elegance and could be worn successfully on a date night. It is that good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1891107"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1891107#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1890019" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Obv the AR is more velvety and richer but I'm sniffing them two next to each other now and they are veeeery similar! Before you spend so much money on AR I would suggest getting the RR cheapie and seeing how you feel in such scent, they are both very sweet and dense. RR leans more towards Baccarat typical sweetness, whereas AR leans more towards Delina (like a dense winter version). AR also reminds me of Rose 01 from Swiss Arabian in the dry down (totally recommend!).<br />
To me, AR is veeeeeery different from Lattafa Amethyst - I don't recommend the latter, it has that horrible cheap oud and musk and is very cheap-smelling and irritating, like a synthetic jam. I might be swapping it for the new Alhambra version - Infini Rose.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-31">05/31/23 04:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Atomic Rose is a very sweet and appealing interpretation of rose. It opens with bright white florals of hedoine and jasmine, accompanied by pink pepper and bergamot before a sweet and soft rose takes over as the leading note. <br />
<br />
There’s a hint of vanilla on top of an ambery base, however the rose remains the main star and doesn’t change all too much throughout the life of the scent. I don’t find the rose to smell very realistic, it comes across more synthetic however I find this with the majority of notes in Initio’s releases. <br />
<br />
It’s a very pleasant fragrance if you enjoy a sweet overdose of rose however there isn’t too much else going. It’s a simplistic scent that’s easy to wear, however lacks character and doesn’t warrant the high price tag unfortunately.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1845681"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1845681#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1838969" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1832792" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="scentifulicious"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1251124"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1251124.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="scentifulicious" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Sospiro-Perfumes/Dolce-Melodia-81490.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81490.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dolce Melodia"title="Dolce Melodia"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1832792ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1832792" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1251124">scentifulicious</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-14">05/14/23 08:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I wore atomic Rose last night as a spring evening scent.  Temperature was around 70 Fahrenheit with high humidity. The occasion was meeting friends to walk the shops along main street of a nearby town (main drag consisting of small boutiques and restaurants) before eating dinner. We all wore dresses to celebrate our (ages around mid 30s) mom's evening out.<br />
<br />
As I sprayed this I was really enjoying what came across to me as a deep, fruity rose scent. Instead of being a young and sweet fruity rose, however, there was a depth and sophistication that made me feel confident. It settled as I drove the 25 minutes to get to the town we were all meeting in. <br />
<br />
As I neared my destination, I noticed and airy sweetness to the quality of my scent bubble that made me think of br 540. The depth of florals I continued to pick up on had me telling myself,  "Stop it! Not everything smells like br540. You're better than that!"<br />
<br />
Until... we entered a small boutique with a selective section of clothing and jewelry, and the owner commented how wonderful I smelled and asked what I was wearing and where I got. After I shared that my scent was atomic Rose from Max aroma, she stated I smelled like br540. <br />
<br />
In my world, hardly anyone wears fragrance, let alone has knowledge of niche fragrances. So part of me was caught off guard that she had any awareness of br540, and although I did understand how the projection bore a resemblance in the air, I was also disappointed that atomic Rose didn't stand out as different (when I do think it is not the same). <br />
<br />
People who don't like br540 may find similar qualities in atomic Rose that makes them not like this one. To me, they are very different and not redundant. I know atomic Rose is more closely compared to delina, and it is similar without the tart sharpness.<br />
<br />
If I had to use other popular scents to describe atomic Rose, a cross between delina and br540 works to capture the protection, but lacks the detail of the scents nuances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1732593">Brownsugarx78</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-06">05/06/23 01:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So first off I do not like Rose scents, but after receiving a sample of another rose perfume I decided to give it a go after reading the reviews. I purchased a 10ml sample from the Initio website. I absolutely do not regret it at all. I was expecting to hate it but I love it. You need to be careful how much you spray as it is powerful. The rose smells like an actual real rose. On first spray it's a pure heavy rose with a heavy bergamot which I did not like at the very start (the bergamot was the dislike at the start), but after a 30 minutes it starts to tone down to a creamy jammy rose and the bergamot seems to fade into the background. You then start to smell the vanilla come through. I find it to be very powdery on my skin, but a very creamy rose enveloped in vanilla, well blended and just beautiful.  It lasts all day even after a heavy gym session. I only used one spray on my neck so it could perform even better with another spray. It leaves a trail everywhere, it definitely does not dry to a skin scent like most others. For me its something néw and different in my collection and I am more than happy to keep it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1826084"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1826084#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1822367" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1803176"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1803176#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1802745" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1448774">BDDII</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-20">03/20/23 18:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is an incredible perfume. It is similar to Delina by Parfums de Marley, but much better in my opinion. Delina is a very safe, overly sweet, one dimensional rose fragrance. This on the other hand is more brooding, mysterious, seductive, and perhaps a bit more mature as well. I do think men can wear this, but it leans very feminine so confidence is key. This is a dark, gorgeous, ambery, musky, vanillic jammy rose with a bit of a jasmine edge. It performs monstrously so don't overspray. I only have one problem with this perfume; the price is quite high, and that would indicate that natural rose has been used in the formulation. They even go so far as to mention Turkish and Bulgarian rose in the notes breakdown, however in my opinion this does not contain any natural rose, at least not enough to detect. Rather, this seems like a very high quality assimilation of natural rose using aroma chemicals. For that reason I think it is quite overpriced. Undoubtedly it smells amazing and performs fantasticly, but the price is still not quite justifiable. That said, there are some great alternatives from Lataffa and the like that get the job done if you don't want to shell out for this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1668533">Luckyeights86</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-01-27">01/27/23 08:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just received my sample of this yesterday and immediately tried it. Maybe my sample was bad?<br />
The opening was gorgeous. Instant fresh, blooming, intoxicating rose. A few minutes after, I noticed a fairly intense metallic/salty smell, which at first I enjoyed and almost made me want to lick my skin, but it soon became the only other note I could detect, and it lasts FOREVER. I really liked this fragrance for the first 15-20 minutes, and after that, it so strongly smelled of bloody, almost scratchy rose that I felt the need to wash it off. Which I couldn't because it's lasting power is insane. Even after I washed it off last night, I can still smell it on my skin at 11am the next day. I couldn't detect any other notes, like the vanilla that is supposedly in the base. I wish I could, because I loved the opening so much, and feel if it even had a whisper of sweetness to it, I might still be able to enjoy the salty metal smell. I can't decide if I should order another sample and see if it's better, or just write it off completely. I initially loved the dark sexy rose I got. Usually my skin brings out the sweetness in fragrances, so I don't know what happened. Very disappointed this one didn't wow me like I expected.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1744984"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1744984#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1742312" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

So, I have unfortunately turned down a lot of Rose scents not really giving them a chance.  To me Delina and Delina Excl smell like toilet water (I'm sorry I tried both multiple times).  I don't get the hype and I feel like a lot of women love it because it's pink and pretty. lol<br />
<br />

This is Tiziana Terenzi' "Delox" on the dry down.  I compared the notes and yep both share some middle and dry down notes.  I love Delox!  This is a Rosey Delox to me and I'm absolutely......loving....every....second....of...it.  Searching for a bottle now on a deal cuz I'm cheap. <br />
<br />

For me it's nice if someone smells a frag on me but the creme de la creme is me oozing sex kitten because the bubble of the fragrance has engulfed and altered my spirit and attitude. I smelled Atomic Rose all day, kept snifffing my everything.  Ugh its good good.  The way I determine if the fragrance is a winner is when my partner leans in and you hear him moan "mmmm...." padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1709179" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ninamariah"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1588494.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ninamariah" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Roja-Dove/Isola-Sol-91214.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.91214.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Isola Sol"title="Isola Sol"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1709179ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1709179" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494">Ninamariah</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-14">12/14/22 10:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>1. INITIO ATOMIC ROSE: Nicely blended rose and vanilla, but so synthetic and cloying, the quality is poor. Not too sweet, not too much rose. The most unisex of all these perfumes mentioned. This is not the worth of money. There is many great options instead of this one.<br />
2. MFK OSM: Again another rose-vanilla -scent (I like that combination, don't get me wrong). This is the strongest one of these all scents which you maybe should sample before your decision to buy FB. This scent is the beast and you definitely doesn't have to re-spray it during the day. This has all in the balance: vanilla, rose, oud and powdery accords. This I found out a little bit synthetic in the beginning and I was thinking this is not for me but this is really addictive, gorgeous scent. After few days I fell in love. Some people say that they find out oud too loud but I think it's really not. It's not like real Oud anyway, it's very western Oud. Anyway this whole scent is loud, in everything and this is in the same time the most unique I think. I will compare these few same kind of scents (or better: the scents which are in the same category) because I find it useful while trying to choose new scents for testing or even blind buys. I don't recommend bb for anyone even if I have many successful blind buys.<br />
<br />
For some people these are maybe similar but for me these all are different! It’s like if you like a lot leopard print you find all leopard print different.<br />
<br />
3. Mancera Roses Vanille<br />
Sorry but again Mancera did it in very synthetical way. If you have a budget you can go for it, it's nice anyway but if you can invest more money then you should definitely choose Xerjoff's K'Bridge Club or stronger scent MFK Oud Satin Mood. Even Tiziana Terenzi's Delox is this same "note family" like as well Initio's Atomic Rose and Delox is really good. If you prefer this kind of scent to be more vanilla and not so much rose and you want something cheaper this is your choice. In the opening I got rose as well but it fades away immediately after 15 minutes. This is just sweet vanilla, not so powdery either like MFK Oud Satin Mood is. This is not so strong and you have to spray many times during a day. Base notes are vanilla and musk. More affordable than others. (Maybe you want to test Montale Cafe Intense as well, very same kind of with a hint of a coffee.)<br />
4. Xerjoff K'Bridge Club<br />
If you prefer good combination of vanilla and rose. Very nicely blended good quality scent but this is quite weak scent compared to Tiziana Terenzi's Delox or MFK Oud Satin Mood. Vanilla and rose is anyway more realistic than in Atomic Rose and this is not so synthetic nor cloying.  Beautiful scent for the office or everywhere when it's polite to think other people and how they will react to your scent. This is sophisticated version of vanilla and rose. This is a little bit fruity (like TT as well) compared to MFK OSM or Initio Atomic Rose. This is more vanilla and more sweet compared to Atomic Rose.<br />
5. Tiziana Terenzi Delox<br />
Stronger projection than Xerjoff K'Bridge Club, but anyway those two are the most similar to each other. Both has some hint of fruits as well and both are really vanilla. If you want to compare these to Initio's Atomic Rose TT has a coffee note with better quality and Atomic Rose is not so sweet, it's most unisex of these all and it's the most synthetic one. Delox is a good quality and long lasting scent. So coffee note you can find from this and Montale Cafe Intense (where the name is miss leading because the coffee note is weak) but I wouldn't compare these as a similar scents, there is too many separating things but if you just look the notes, those two look so similar. This is musk and amber based. I love this TT's Delox! This I definitely want a full bottle.<br />
<br />
Despite what is the base notes here you can find these really similar scents. But since we all are different and we experience the scents so different ways I just recommend to sample all of these and decide after that. Or you can find yourself in the situation like me wanting almost all of those because I find so unique things between these as well. Mancera and Montale I don't like to have nor Atomic Rose. Too synthetic for me. Since I blind bought MFK OSM and fell in love with that I would like to have as well some more "shy" scent from rose-vanilla -combo. I think I will buy FB of Delox or I try to find some very natural Rose Vanilla.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1709179"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1709179#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1708167" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1141379">AndySmellsGreat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-11-28">11/28/19 01:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Phwwooooooooaaaaarrrrrrrrrrr!<br />
<br />
Another absolute bowl you over scent from Initio.<br />
<br />
In the vain of Side Effect - just replace fruit, cinnamon and spice notes with Rose.<br />
<br />
Somewhat bright Rose with what smells like crushed petals given depth with a sultry amber base. Just enough depth so as not to make it a winter scent only but indeed an all year round scent.<br />
<br />
Performance in longevity and Sillage that in this class has very few equals. People will smell it miles away and ask, they will know it’s not a cheap perfume.<br />
<br />
Ironically I am not at all a Floral let alone especially a Rose fan but when I saw it released I ordered a sample just because it was Initio and today the full bottle arrived.<br />
<br />
Worth E V E R Y single cent! Hah - now I like Rose scents lol</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1119702"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1119702#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2242573" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1226157" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="emerson10"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1238550"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="emerson10" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/ALTAIA/Don-t-Cry-For-Me-32343.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.32343.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Don't Cry For Me"title="Don't Cry For Me"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1226157ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1226157" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1238550">emerson10</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-09-18">09/18/20 22:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After all the positive reviews I've seen raving about this as the most irresistible/seductive fragrance, I could not wait to try it.<br />
<br />
And with the first spray I was not disappointed. I literally said out loud, "YES!" It was the rose for the non-rose fan. I'm not anti-rose, I just generally don't gravitate towards strong rose fragrances. This was the sexiest rose ever - sophisticated and modern, expensive and sexy. And while rose is the most dominant note, it's definitely not a single note perfume. And with that...<br />
<br />
That's when part 2 (and every subsequent part of this fragrance set in). I totally agree with other reviewers here about the metallic note that sets in. Within 15 mins, I was getting Crayola vibes, and within an hour the Crayola transitioned to pencil shavings.<br />
<br />
<br />
Once you smell the crayon/pencil shavings, you cannot unsmell them. Basically smelled like the most beautiful pencil case ever (and there's really no adjective you can put in front on pencil case that will make me want to smell like a pencil case). <br />
<br />
WHO I PICTURE THIS ON:<br />
a sex robot? It's like sexy, but synthetic/mechanical.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1226157"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1226157#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1709179" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1709179" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ninamariah"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1588494.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ninamariah" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Roja-Dove/Isola-Sol-91214.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.91214.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Isola Sol"title="Isola Sol"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1709179ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1709179" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494">Ninamariah</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-14">12/14/22 10:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>1. INITIO ATOMIC ROSE: Nicely blended rose and vanilla, but so synthetic and cloying, the quality is poor. Not too sweet, not too much rose. The most unisex of all these perfumes mentioned. This is not the worth of money. There is many great options instead of this one.<br />
2. MFK OSM: Again another rose-vanilla -scent (I like that combination, don't get me wrong). This is the strongest one of these all scents which you maybe should sample before your decision to buy FB. This scent is the beast and you definitely doesn't have to re-spray it during the day. This has all in the balance: vanilla, rose, oud and powdery accords. This I found out a little bit synthetic in the beginning and I was thinking this is not for me but this is really addictive, gorgeous scent. After few days I fell in love. Some people say that they find out oud too loud but I think it's really not. It's not like real Oud anyway, it's very western Oud. Anyway this whole scent is loud, in everything and this is in the same time the most unique I think. I will compare these few same kind of scents (or better: the scents which are in the same category) because I find it useful while trying to choose new scents for testing or even blind buys. I don't recommend bb for anyone even if I have many successful blind buys.<br />
<br />
For some people these are maybe similar but for me these all are different! It’s like if you like a lot leopard print you find all leopard print different.<br />
<br />
3. Mancera Roses Vanille<br />
Sorry but again Mancera did it in very synthetical way. If you have a budget you can go for it, it's nice anyway but if you can invest more money then you should definitely choose Xerjoff's K'Bridge Club or stronger scent MFK Oud Satin Mood. Even Tiziana Terenzi's Delox is this same "note family" like as well Initio's Atomic Rose and Delox is really good. If you prefer this kind of scent to be more vanilla and not so much rose and you want something cheaper this is your choice. In the opening I got rose as well but it fades away immediately after 15 minutes. This is just sweet vanilla, not so powdery either like MFK Oud Satin Mood is. This is not so strong and you have to spray many times during a day. Base notes are vanilla and musk. More affordable than others. (Maybe you want to test Montale Cafe Intense as well, very same kind of with a hint of a coffee.)<br />
4. Xerjoff K'Bridge Club<br />
If you prefer good combination of vanilla and rose. Very nicely blended good quality scent but this is quite weak scent compared to Tiziana Terenzi's Delox or MFK Oud Satin Mood. Vanilla and rose is anyway more realistic than in Atomic Rose and this is not so synthetic nor cloying.  Beautiful scent for the office or everywhere when it's polite to think other people and how they will react to your scent. This is sophisticated version of vanilla and rose. This is a little bit fruity (like TT as well) compared to MFK OSM or Initio Atomic Rose. This is more vanilla and more sweet compared to Atomic Rose.<br />
5. Tiziana Terenzi Delox<br />
Stronger projection than Xerjoff K'Bridge Club, but anyway those two are the most similar to each other. Both has some hint of fruits as well and both are really vanilla. If you want to compare these to Initio's Atomic Rose TT has a coffee note with better quality and Atomic Rose is not so sweet, it's most unisex of these all and it's the most synthetic one. Delox is a good quality and long lasting scent. So coffee note you can find from this and Montale Cafe Intense (where the name is miss leading because the coffee note is weak) but I wouldn't compare these as a similar scents, there is too many separating things but if you just look the notes, those two look so similar. This is musk and amber based. I love this TT's Delox! This I definitely want a full bottle.<br />
<br />
Despite what is the base notes here you can find these really similar scents. But since we all are different and we experience the scents so different ways I just recommend to sample all of these and decide after that. Or you can find yourself in the situation like me wanting almost all of those because I find so unique things between these as well. Mancera and Montale I don't like to have nor Atomic Rose. Too synthetic for me. Since I blind bought MFK OSM and fell in love with that I would like to have as well some more "shy" scent from rose-vanilla -combo. I think I will buy FB of Delox or I try to find some very natural Rose Vanilla.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1709179"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1709179#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1177984" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
