padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1239118">RosieRose16</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-05-20">05/20/20 06:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought a small sample of Atomic Rose based on the strength of all of the reviews I have seen and the fact that most of the notes &amp; accords are ones that I tend to enjoy, but honestly, this is one of the worst things I have ever smelt. <br />
<br />
I know it is strong so I just used a small amount - maybe 0.5ml from my sample and it made me gag instantly. Within a hour I had a headache and was feeling sick - I was waiting it out to see if it would mellow but after about 2 hours I had to take a shower and scrub it off as much as I could. It felt like I was in a cloud of something tangy and dirty smelling. It has now been 30 hours since I initially sprayed it and 28 since I showered it off, I have had another shower in between and sprayed a different perfume AND I CAN STILL SMELL ATOMIC ROSE! <br />
<br />
Clearly there is something about it that just doesn't agree with me - perhaps the hedione as that isn't something I have smelt before? I do generally get good longevity out of most perfumes - I can easily get 12 hours out a Jo Malone EDC for example so maybe it is my skin? <br />
<br />
Now, 30 hours later I can smell a hit of rose but it still mostly smells tangy. <br />
<br />
Oddly, my husband thought it smelt amazing and kept sniffing at me all day - he did however say that whatever room I was in, as soon as he walked in you could smell it - even after I showered.<br />
<br />
Obviously others really like it so I am sure it has good qualities - I am disappointed that it doesn't work for me as I wanted something a bit special but never mind - the search continues!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1177984"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1177984#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1223268" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1223268" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Binchicken"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1251454"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1251454.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Binchicken" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Mizensir/Poudre-d-Or-48660.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48660.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Poudre d'Or"title="Poudre d'Or"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1223268ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1223268" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1251454">Binchicken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-09-12">09/12/20 00:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On me this is a metallic sweet rose with HUGE projection and excellent longevity. I ordered this sample at the same time as Delina, sure that I would love one or the other. Nope. The metallic note is unpleasant to my nose, reminds me a little of blood, and removes any realism that might have saved the rose for me. <br />
<br />
In saying that, I think this would be an excellent option to wear out clubbing, for both men and women. It does smell expensive and sexy, is clearly fantastic quality, and people across the room will be able to smell you. If I smelt a man wearing this in the club, I would be drawn to him. If he wore it running errands, I would be turned off. I think its a very situational fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="57587"comment_id="1223268"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Atomic-Rose-57587.html?ccid=1223268#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1277041" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
